file.\n    75→\n    76→    Reads the file, finds the first ``^---`` line, and removes everything before\n    77→    it.  Uses atomic write (write to ``.tmp`` then ``os.replace()``) to prevent\n    78→    partial file states.\n    79→\n    80→    Returns the byte count of the stripped preamble (0 when file already starts\n    81→    with ``---`` or no frontmatter delimiter is found).\n    82→    \"\"\"\n    83→    import os\n    84→    import re\n    85→\n    86→    try:\n    87→        content = output_file.read_text(encoding=\"utf-8\")\n    88→    except FileNotFoundError:\n    89→        return 0\n    90→\n    91→    # Already starts with frontmatter delimiter -- nothing to strip\n    92→    if content.lstrip().startswith(\"---\"):\n    93→        return 0\n    94→\n    95→    # Search for the first ^--- line\n    96→    match = re.search(r\"^---[ \\t]*$\", content, re.MULTILINE)\n    97→    if match is None:\n    98→        # No frontmatter found at all -- leave file unchanged\n    99→        return 0\n   100→\n   101→    preamble = content[: match.start()]\n   102→    cleaned = content[match.start() :]\n   103→    preamble_bytes = len(preamble.encode(\"utf-8\"))\n   104→\n   105→    # Atomic write: tmp file + os.replace\n   106→    tmp_file = output_file.with_suffix(output_file.suffix + \".tmp\")\n   107→    tmp_file.write_text(cleaned, encoding=\"utf-8\")\n   108→    os.replace(tmp_file, output_file)\n   109→\n   110→    _log.info(\"Stripped %d-byte preamble from %s\", preamble_bytes, output_file)\n   111→    return preamble_bytes\n   112→\n   113→\n   114→def _inject_pipeline_diagnostics(\n   115→    output_file: Path,\n   116→    started_at: datetime,\n   117→    finished_at: datetime,\n   118→) -> None:\n   119→    \"\"\"Inject executor-populated pipeline_diagnostics into extraction frontmatter.\n   120→\n   121→    The LLM cannot reliably produce execution timing or environment metadata,\n   122→    so the executor injects these fields post-subprocess (FR-033).\n   123→    \"\"\"\n   124→    content = output_file.read_text(encoding=\"utf-8\")\n   125→    if not content.startswith(\"---\"):\n   126→        return\n   127→\n   128→    # Find end of frontmatter\n   129→    end_idx = content.find(\"\\n---\", 3)\n   130→    if end_idx == -1:\n   131→        return\n   132→\n   133→    elapsed = (finished_at - started_at).total_seconds()\n   134→    diagnostics_line = (\n   135→        f\"pipeline_diagnostics: \"\n   136→        f\"{{elapsed_seconds: {elapsed:.1f}, \"\n   137→        f\"started_at: \\\"{started_at.isoformat()}\\\", \"\n   138→        f\"finished_at: \\\"{finished_at.isoformat()}\\\"}}\"\n   139→    )\n   140→\n   141→    # Insert before the closing ---\n   142→    new_content = (\n   143→        content[: end_idx]\n   144→        + \"\\n\"\n   145→        + diagnostics_line\n   146→        + content[end_idx:]\n   147→    )\n   148→    output_file.write_text(new_content, encoding=\"utf-8\")\n   149→\n   150→\n   151→def roadmap_run_step(\n   152→    step: Step,\n   153→    config: PipelineConfig,\n   154→    cancel_check: Callable[[], bool],\n   155→) -> StepResult:\n   156→    \"\"\"Execute a single roadmap step as a Claude subprocess.\n   157→\n   158→    Builds argv with context isolation, launches process, waits with\n   159→    timeout, and returns StepResult.\n   160→    \"\"\"\n   161→    started_at = datetime.now(timezone.utc)\n   162→\n   163→    if config.dry_run:\n   164→        _log.info(\"[dry-run] Would execute step '%s'\", step.id)\n   165→        return StepResult(\n   166→            step=step,\n   167→            status=StepStatus.PASS,\n   168→            attempt=1,\n   169→            started_at=started_at,\n   170→            finished_at=datetime.now(timezone.utc),\n   171→        )\n   172→\n   173→    # Inline embedding: read input files into the prompt instead of --file flags\n   174→    embedded = _embed_inputs(step.inputs)\n   175→    if embedded and len(embedded.encode(\"utf-8\")) <= _EMBED_SIZE_LIMIT:\n   176→        effective_prompt = step.prompt + \"\\n\\n\" + embedded\n   177→        extra_args: list[str] = []\n   178→    elif embedded:\n   179→        _log.warning(\n   180→            \"Step '%s': embedded inputs exceed %d bytes, falling back to --file flags\",\n   181→            step.id,\n   182→            _EMBED_SIZE_LIMIT,\n   183→        )\n   184→        effective_prompt = step.prompt\n   185→        extra_args = [\n   186→            arg\n   187→            for input_path in step.inputs\n   188→            for arg in (\"--file\", str(input_path))\n   189→        ]\n   190→    else:\n   191→        effective_prompt = step.prompt\n   192→        extra_args = []\n   193→\n   194→    proc = ClaudeProcess(\n   195→        prompt=effective_prompt,\n   196→        output_file=step.output_file,\n   197→        error_file=step.output_file.with_suffix(\".err\"),\n   198→        max_turns=config.max_turns,\n   199→        model=step.model or config.model,\n   200→        permission_flag=config.permission_flag,\n   201→        timeout_seconds=step.timeout_seconds,\n   202→        output_format=\"text\",\n   203→        extra_args=extra_args,\n   204→    )\n   205→\n   206→    proc.start()\n   207→\n   208→    # Poll for cancellation while waiting\n   209→    while proc._process is not None and proc._process.poll() is None:\n   210→        if cancel_check():\n   211→            proc.terminate()\n   212→            return StepResult(\n   213→                step=step,\n   214→                status=StepStatus.CANCELLED,\n   215→                attempt=1,\n   216→                gate_failure_reason=\"Cancelled by external signal\",\n   217→                started_at=started_at,\n   218→                finished_at=datetime.now(timezone.utc),\n   219→            )\n   220→        time.sleep(1)\n   221→\n   222→    exit_code = proc.wait()\n   223→    finished_at = datetime.now(timezone.utc)\n   224→\n   225→    if exit_code == 124:\n   226→        return StepResult(\n   227→            step=step,\n   228→            status=StepStatus.TIMEOUT,\n   229→            attempt=1,\n   230→            gate_failure_reason=f\"Step '{step.id}' timed out after {step.timeout_seconds}s\",\n   231→            started_at=started_at,\n   232→            finished_at=finished_at,\n   233→        )\n   234→\n   235→    if exit_code != 0:\n   236→        return StepResult(\n   237→            step=step,\n   238→            status=StepStatus.FAIL,\n   239→            attempt=1,\n   240→            gate_failure_reason=f\"Step '{step.id}' exited with code {exit_code}\",\n   241→            started_at=started_at,\n   242→            finished_at=finished_at,\n   243→        )\n   244→\n   245→    # Sanitize output: strip conversational preamble before gate validation\n   246→    _sanitize_output(step.output_file)\n   247→\n   248→    # Inject executor-populated fields into extract step frontmatter (FR-033)\n   249→    if step.id == \"extract\" and step.output_file.exists():\n   250→        _inject_pipeline_diagnostics(step.output_file, started_at, finished_at)\n   251→\n   252→    # Process completed successfully; gate check happens in execute_pipeline\n   253→    return StepResult(\n   254→        step=step,\n   255→        status=StepStatus.PASS,\n   256→        attempt=1,\n   257→        started_at=started_at,\n   258→        finished_at=finished_at,\n   259→    )\n   260→\n   261→\n   262→def build_certify_step(\n   263→    config: RoadmapConfig,\n   264→    findings: list | None = None,\n   265→    context_sections: dict[str, str] | None = None,\n   266→) -> Step:\n   267→    \"\"\"Build a certify Step for execution via execute_pipeline().\n   268→\n   269→    The certify step runs as a standard Step (not ClaudeProcess directly)\n   270→    per spec section 2.5. Uses atomic write (write to ``.tmp`` then ``os.replace()``) to prevent\n    partial file states.\n\n    Returns the byte count of the stripped preamble (0 when file already starts\n    with ``---`` or no frontmatter delimiter is found).\n    \"\"\"\n    import os\n    import re\n\n    try:\n        content = output_file.read_text(encoding=\"utf-8\")\n    except FileNotFoundError:\n        return 0\n\n    # back to --file flags\n_EMBED_SIZE_LIMIT = 100 * 1024  # 100 KB\n\n\ndef _embed_inputs(input_paths: list[Path]) -> str:\n    \"\"\"Read input files and return their contents as fenced code blocks.\n\n    Each file is wrapped in a fenced block with a ``# <path>`` header.\n    Returns an empty string when *input_paths* is empty (no-op).\n    \"\"\"\n    if not input_paths:\n        return \"\"\n\n first ``^---`` line, and removes everything before\n    it.  Uses atomic write (write to ``.tmp`` then ``os.replace()``) to prevent\n    partial file states.\n\n    Returns the byte count of the stripped preamble (0 when file already starts\n    with ``---`` or no frontmatter delimiter is found).\n    \"\"\"\n    import os\n    import re\n\n    try:\n        content = output_file.read_text(encoding=\"utf-8\")\n    except FileNotFoundError:\n        return 0\n\n    # Already starts with frontmatter delimiter -- nothing to strip\n    if content.lstrip().startswith(\"---\"):\n        return 0\n\n    # Search for the first ^--- line\n    match = re.search(r\"^---[ \\t]*$\", content, re.MULTILINE)\n    if match is None:\n        # No frontmatter found at all -- leave file unchanged\n        return 0\n\n    preamble = content[: match.start()]\n    cleaned = content[match.start() :]\n    preamble_bytes = len(preamble.encode(\"utf-8\"))\n\n    # Atomic write: tmp file + os.replace\n    tmp_file = output_file.with_suffix(output_file.suffix + \".tmp\")\n    tmp_file.write_text(cleaned, encoding=\"utf-8\")\n    os.replace(tmp_file, output_file)\n\n    _log.info(\"Stripped %d-byte preamble from %s\", preamble_bytes, output_file)\n    return preamble_bytes\n\n\ndef _inject_pipeline_diagnostics(\n    output_file: Path,\n    started_at: datetime,\n    finished_at: datetime,\n) -> None:\n    \"\"\"Inject executor-populated pipeline_diagnostics into extraction frontmatter.\n\n    The LLM cannot reliably produce execution timing or environment metadata,\n    so the executor injects these fields post-subprocess (FR-033).\n    \"\"\"\n    content = output_file.read_text(encoding=\"utf-8\")\n    if not content.startswith(\"---\"):\n        return\n\n    # Insert before the closing ---\n    new_content = (\n        content[: end_idx]\n        + \"\\n\"\n        + diagnostics_line\n        + content[end_idx:]\n    )\n    output_file.write_text(new_content, encoding=\"utf-8\")\n\n\ndef roadmap_run_step(\n    step: Step,\n    config: PipelineConfig,\n    cancel_check: Callable[[], bool],\n) -> StepResult:\n    \"\"\"Execute a single roadmap step as a Claude subprocess.\n\n    Builds argv with context isolation, launches process, waits with\n    timeout, and returns StepResult.\n    \"\"\"\n    started_at = datetime.now(timezone.utc)\n\n    if config.dry_run:\n        _log.info(\"[dry-run] Would execute step '%s'\", step.id)\n        return StepResult(\n            step=step,\n            status=StepStatus.PASS,\n            attempt=1,\n            started_at=started_at,\n            finished_at=datetime.now(timezone.utc),\n        )\n\n    # Inline embedding: read input files into the prompt instead of --file flags\n    embedded = _embed_inputs(step.inputs)\n    if embedded and len(embedded.encode(\"utf-8\")) <= _EMBED_SIZE_LIMIT:\n        effective_prompt = step.prompt + \"\\n\\n\" + embedded\n        extra_args: list[str] = []\n    elif embedded:\n        _log.warning(\n            \"Step '%s': embedded inputs exceed %d bytes, falling back to --file flags\",\n            step.id,\n            _EMBED_SIZE_LIMIT,\n        )\n        effective_prompt = step.prompt\n        extra_args = [\n            arg\n            for input_path in step.inputs\n            for arg in (\"--file\", str(input_path))\n        ]\n    else:\n        effective_prompt = step.prompt\n        extra_args = []\n\n    proc = ClaudeProcess(\n        prompt=effective_prompt,\n        output_file=step.output_file,\n        error_file=step.output_file.with_suffix(\".err\"),\n        max_turns=config.max_turns,\n        model=step.model or config.model,\n        permission_flag=config.permission_flag,\n        timeout_seconds=step.timeout_seconds,\n        output_format=\"text\",\n        extra_args=extra_args,\n    )\n\n    proc.start()\n\n    # Poll for cancellation while waiting\n    while proc._process is not None and proc._process.poll() is None:\n        if cancel_check():\n            proc.terminate()\n            return StepResult(\n                step=step,\n                status=StepStatus.CANCELLED,\n                attempt=1,\n                gate_failure_reason=\"Cancelled by external signal\",\n                started_at=started_at,\n                finished_at=datetime.now(timezone.utc),\n            )\n        time.sleep(1)\n\n    exit_code = proc.wait()\n    finished_at = datetime.now(timezone.utc)\n\n    if exit_code == 124:\n        return StepResult(\n            step=step,\n            status=StepStatus.TIMEOUT,\n            attempt=1,\n            gate_failure_reason=f\"Step '{step.id}' timed out after {step.timeout_seconds}s\",\n            started_at=started_at,\n            finished_at=finished_at,\n        )\n\n    if exit_code != 0:\n        return StepResult(\n            step=step,\n            status=StepStatus.FAIL,\n            attempt=1,\n            gate_failure_reason=f\"Step '{step.id}' exited with code {exit_code}\",\n            started_at=started_at,\n            finished_at=finished_at,\n        )\n\n    # Sanitize output: strip conversational preamble before gate validation\n    _sanitize_output(step.output_file)\n\n    # Inject executor-populated fields into extract step frontmatter (FR-033)\n    if step.id == \"extract\" and step.output_file.exists():\n        _inject_pipeline_diagnostics(step.output_file, started_at, finished_at)\n\n    # Process completed successfully; gate check happens in execute_pipeline\n    return StepResult(\n        step=step,\n        status=StepStatus.PASS,\n        attempt=1,\n        started_at=started_at,\n        finished_at=finished_at,\n    )\n\n\ndef build_certify_step(\n    config: RoadmapConfig,\n    findings: list | None = None,\n    context_sections: dict[str, str] | None = None,\n) -> Step:\n    \"\"\"Build a certify Step for execution via execute_pipeline().\n\n    The certify step runs as a standard Step (not ClaudeProcess directly)\n    per spec section 2.5. config.output_dir\n    certification_report = out / \"certification-report.md\"\n\n    prompt = build_certification_prompt(\n        findings=findings or [],\n        context_sections=context_sections or {},\n    )\n\n    return Step(\n        id=\"certify\",\n        prompt=prompt,\n        output_file=certification_report,\n        gate=CERTIFY_GATE,\n        timeout_seconds=300,\n        inputs=[out / \"remediation-tasklist.md\"],\n        retry_limit=1,\n    )\n\n\ndef _build_steps(config: RoadmapConfig) -> list[Step | list[Step]]:\n    \"\"\"Build the 9-step pipeline with parallel \"\"\"Format HALT diagnostic output per spec section 6.2.\"\"\"\n    failed = [r for r in results if r.status in (StepStatus.FAIL, StepStatus.TIMEOUT)]\n    passed = [r for r in results if r.status == derive_pipeline_status(state: dict) -> str:\n    \"\"\"Derive the overall pipeline status from state transitions.\n\n    State transitions at each boundary:\n    - post-validate: validated | None:\n    \"\"\"Execute the roadmap generation pipeline.\n\n    Builds the step list, handles --dry-run and --resume, then\n    delegates to execute_pipeline() with roadmap_run_step.\n\n    After all 9 steps pass, auto-invokes validation unless\n    --no-validate is set or --resume halted on a failed step.\n\n    Note: --no-validate does NOT skip the spec-fidelity step\n    (FR-010, AC-005). It only skips the post-pipeline validation\n    subsystem.\n    \"\"\"\n    config.output_dir.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)\n\n    steps = _build_steps(config)\n\n    # --dry-run: print plan and gate_passed\n\n        steps = _apply_resume(steps, config, gate_passed)\n\n    # Execute pipeline\n    results = execute_pipeline(\n        steps=steps,\n        config=config,\n failures\n    failures = [r for r in results if r.status in (StepStatus.FAIL, StepStatus.TIMEOUT)]\n    if failures:\n        halt_msg = _format_halt_output(results, config)\n        print(halt_msg, file=sys.stderr)\n        sys.exit(1)\n\n    print(f\"\\n[roadmap] Pipeline complete: {len(results)} steps passed\", flush=True)\n\n    # Auto-invoke validation after successful pipeline completion\n already completed (--resume path)\n    if resume:\n        state_file = config.output_dir / \".roadmap-state.json\"\n        state = read_state(state_file)\n        if state and \"validation\" in state:\n            saved = state[\"validation\"]\n            if saved.get(\"status\") in (\"pass\", \"fail\"):\n                print(\n                    f\"[roadmap] Validation already completed RoadmapConfig,\n    gate_fn: Callable,\n) -> list[Step | list[Step]]:\n    \"\"\"Apply --resume logic: skip steps whose outputs already pass gates.\n\n    Also checks for stale spec detection.\n
